Current Affairs Commentary

Renewed Tension in the Arms Race (Cautious)

Switzerland is a sacred haven of peace in Europe and a model for democratic countries worldwide. Recently, due to the deepening global economic crisis, even this renowned "world park," Switzerland, has lost its former prosperity. Those who once flocked to its picturesque landscapes for leisurely pursuits have also seen their interest wane with the economic downturn. Unexpectedly, today, this universally recognized paradise is known for expanding its military. Since the arms reduction conference broke down, Germany withdrew from the League of Nations, and Italy expressed dissent, European countries have felt increasingly uneasy. Nations directly in the line of fire, such as Germany, France, and even smaller countries like China, have all been striving to expand their military and actively promote the military-industrial complex to stimulate the general economic climate and overcome the current difficulties. Even Switzerland, with an area of only 41,000 square kilometers and a population of only 4.1 million, with a standing army of only 25,000, is now, in light of the tense European situation and fearing a renewed conflict between Germany and France, sparing no expense in allocating 80 million Swiss francs to enhance its military. Its military tanks, infantry artillery, and light and heavy machine guns have all been increased. People who have served in the military and received training are also undergoing advanced retraining. From Switzerland, we can gauge the current state of Europe and the degree of urgency.

Since the early days of human society, competition has been more prevalent than peaceful movements. After the formation of national organizations, competition between individuals transformed into antagonism between countries or ethnic groups. The advancement of human society's economy, politics, and culture has largely depended on the continued development in this contradictory state of competition and opposition. After the end of World War I in 1918, all countries, suffering heavy losses, desired rest. Therefore, the call for peace began to be generally accepted worldwide. However, now that advanced countries have developed extreme manufacturing capabilities, domestic consumer markets cannot accommodate the surplus goods. Overseas colonies and markets in underdeveloped countries are shrinking due to competitive dumping. The smaller the market, the fiercer the competition. To maintain old markets, open up new markets, and divide markets with undefined boundaries, powerful countries are all using force as a backing. Overall, the situation is quite similar to the so-called "armed peace" before 1914.

With the rise of military competition, the Army Disarmament Conference inevitably came to a standstill, or even failure. The irreconcilable economic interests of the major powers, France's security guarantees, Germany's military equality, Italy's reform of the League of Nations, and England's traditional diplomacy all clashed with each other. It is very clear that army disarmament cannot find a suitable solution. What about the navy? Currently, only five countries—England, America, Japan, France, and Italy—have the financial resources to expand their navies and a naval power base. Among these five countries, England, America, and Japan have stronger naval forces, making naval agreements seemingly easier to reach. However, the center of the maritime competition for supremacy is in the Pacific Ocean, which falls within the competitive scope of England, America, and Japan. Each wants to maintain its absolute military advantage. The Washington Treaty will expire two years from now. What will the 1935 naval conference be like? Will the naval warship ratio lead to an increase in armaments due to inequality, or will it trigger an armed conflict? We will set aside such a pessimistic outlook for now. Let's analyze the current situation. Assuming that the Second Washington Conference can be convened and that England, America, and Japan can consider the needs of peace and express that all issues are open for discussion, there will still be at least the following difficulties. First, the leadership issue. England and America dominated the previous Washington Conference. In the future, Japan will strive with all its might to seize the hegemony of the Far East. Second, the ship type issue. England has naval ports in colonies all over the world where it can refuel, so it advocates for small ships. Japan's islands are adjacent, and its offensive and defensive targets are not far away, so it can also agree to small ships. America is different. The Atlantic and Pacific Oceans are too far apart, and the Philippines are even 6,000 nautical miles away. Even if it adopts an extremely defensive posture, it needs larger ships to be able to apply them. This argument is difficult to concede. Third, the tonnage of submarines and the limitations of aircraft carriers are also based on different opinions, with no possibility of cooperation. With such a situation in the army and navy competition, can there be hope for world peace?

Demand for Re-armament

France drafts a reply to Germany, rejecting direct negotiations outside the scope of the League of Nations. France and Belgium reach complete understanding.

Germany agrees to compromise on expanding its standing army.

But must sign non-aggression pacts with its neighbors as a condition.

The trial period for supervision is reduced from four years to two years.

(Paris) The French government's memorandum in response to the German government's demand for military equipment was drafted today at a cabinet meeting and will be delivered to the German Ministry of Foreign Affairs by Ambassador Ponsot to Germany within a few days. It is reported that the content indicates that France is willing to continue exchanging opinions through ordinary diplomatic channels, but disarmament negotiations must be conducted in Geneva within the scope of the League of Nations, so that all relevant countries can participate. According to reports, French Prime Minister Doumergue met with the ministers of foreign affairs, army, navy, and air force yesterday to discuss this matter. The cabinet today finalized the results of yesterday's discussion. According to well-informed sources, France is now willing to compromise on the German demand to expand its standing army by 100,000 and its militia by 300,000, agreeing to increase it to 200,000, but on the condition that Germany sign non-aggression treaties with its neighbors. It is also willing to shorten the four-year trial period for monitoring disarmament by two years. It is reported that France's attitude in this memorandum is in accordance with the methods agreed upon in the previous talks between British and French diplomatic authorities. At that time, both parties strictly stipulated that all disarmament discussions must be held within the League of Nations. (National Telegraph, 28th)

British Ambassador to Italy, Drummond, Meets with Simon

Reports Mussolini's opinions

(London) Today, the British Ambassador to Italy, Drummond, went to Capri to arrange a meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Foreign Secretary Simon in the future. Drummond traveled by car from Rome to Naples today and took an Italian torpedo boat to the island of Capri. (Reuters, 27th)

Rome British Ambassador to Italy Sir Drummond's meeting with British Foreign Secretary Simon in Capri is intended to report to Simon Italy's views on reforming the League of Nations and disarmament issues. Regarding the first point, the Roman government is expressing the reactions of several countries. Foreign Vice Minister Suvich's trip to Berlin recently revealed that even if the League of Nations is reorganized, it will not be enough to induce Germany to participate in Geneva again. On the other hand, France clearly advocates reorganizing the League of Nations and consolidating its strength, and the United Kingdom has also expressed its support. In view of this, the Roman government may no longer overthrow the current organization of the League of Nations and reorganize it from scratch. Regarding the issue of armaments, it is known here that the United Kingdom supports Germany's partial rearmament and believes that France can also acknowledge it. What we should pay attention to is that the number of troops demanded by Germany is 300,000, while the UK's disarmament plan stipulates only 200,000. In summary, Simon and Mussolini may seek a compromise basis that is roughly close to British opinion, allowing Germany to rearm to a small extent on the one hand, and requiring France to partially disarm on the other, in order to seek mutual rapprochement between Paris and Berlin. (Havas, 27th)

French Ambassador to Germany Summoned Home

(Paris) French Ambassador to Germany Ponsot arrived in Paris at 11:00 this morning. (Reuters, 28th)

(Paris) Yesterday, the ministers of the army, navy, and air force held a meeting to discuss Franco-German relations, especially the issue of Germany's request to rearm. The Council of State continued to discuss this matter today. After the ministers of the army, navy, and air force presented their opinions, the Council of State decided to send new instructions to French Ambassador to Germany Ponsot, which may be delivered tomorrow or Friday. After the meeting, reporters asked Prime Minister Doumergue for his opinion. Doumergue replied, "As a rule, diplomatic documents cannot be published before they are sent to foreign countries, and the government should strictly maintain secrecy. I hope you can understand that what I can say is only the following: negotiations with various countries are the methods determined by the presidium of the Disarmament Conference. France is willing to negotiate with any relevant country. However, France ultimately believes that disarmament should be carried out within the scope of the League of Nations in order to seek general security. France has put forward various concrete suggestions in this regard, and its attitude has always been the same. Everyone must be able to understand its sincere desire for peace." (Havas, 27th)

France and Germany Still Disagree on Military Security

(London) The Paris correspondent of The Times exclusively stated that the French government's attitude does not imply that continued talks in any form are impossible after exchanging opinions with Germany without any results, nor does it imply that the French government opposes direct Franco-German talks in principle. However, because France and Germany differ too much in their views on military security and the League of Nations, it is believed that negotiations should still be conducted through ordinary diplomatic channels. This will indeed make it difficult to make any progress before the meeting of the Executive Council of the League of Nations in mid-January next year, and it will force the meeting of the Main Committee of the Disarmament Conference to continue to be postponed. (National Telegraph, 28th)

France's Answer is Tantamount to Shifting Responsibility for the Breakup

(London) The British newspapers deeply regretted the French cabinet's rejection of Germany's proposal on disarmament, saying that France's answer was equal to France shifting the responsibility for the breakup of the talks. The Morning Post stated that France is currently unable to solve any diplomatic or political problems. The only hope now lies in the talks between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Foreign Secretary Simon, which can provide a new impetus for discussions between Germany and France. (National Telegraph, 28th)

Franco-Belgian Talks Involve Both Politics and Economy

(Paris) France's attitude towards disarmament and the future of the League of Nations has continued to gain support. Today it was heard that French Foreign Minister Poncet and Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans had reached a complete understanding on the two points that Germany must not rearm and the League of Nations must not be fundamentally reorganized. (Reuters, 27th)

(Paris) The issues discussed by Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans and the French authorities are roughly divided into two types: one is political issues and the other is economic issues. France and Belgium have close relations and common interests, and there will be no differences of opinion during the consultations. Regarding diplomatic issues, both countries regard Germany's military expansion as a danger and do not ignore it. Hymans will probably discuss national defense issues with the Army Chief. Regarding the League of Nations, both France and Belgium believe that the rights of small countries cannot be harmed by anyone. Regarding economic issues, Hymans will explain the following views to Minister of Commerce Laurent-Eynac: since the economic organizations of France and Belgium are the same and both strictly adhere to the gold standard, the two countries should mutually combine on monetary issues to express their economic interdependence. In addition, the issue of France's import restrictions is also on the agenda. Finally, Hymans will discuss issues related to workers on the border between the two countries with former Budget Minister Lamoureux. In other words, the issue of Belgian workers working in France and French workers working in Belgium. (Havas, 27th)

Greek Foreign Minister Runs for Peace in the Balkans

(Paris) Greek Foreign Minister Maximos plans to travel to Rome from abroad on January 2 next year for a short stay, and then go directly to London, and then return to Paris from London. This morning, Mr. Maximos made a statement to our reporter, saying, "We have achieved a very important result in building peace in the Balkan Peninsula, namely the Treaty of Friendship signed between Greece and Turkey. Greece and Turkey are now closely cooperating to achieve this great cause. In the spirit of Balkan peace, I will go to Zagreb, Yugoslavia, to meet with King Alexander of Yugoslavia. When I met with Foreign Minister Poncet yesterday, Poncet deeply agreed with this policy, saying that it was in line with France's efforts for Europe. I will visit the British and Italian authorities in the near future. I know that the governments of the two countries will definitely express their approval of our efforts for peace." (Havas, 27th)

German Newspaper Ridicules the League of Nations for Incompetence

(London) According to news from Berlin, the organ newspaper of the National Socialist Party stated that the League of Nations itself has proven to be a failure. In general, the League of Nations has no result-oriented ability and is not in line with the trend. It also stated that the belief in international conferences was created by the effect of the Lausanne Conference in 1932 and has been destroyed by subsequent conferences. Since the failure of the London Economic Conference, there has been no hope of international solutions in the near future. (Reuters, 27th)

Japanese Ambassador to France Sato Presents Credentials

(Paris) President Lebrun officially received Sato, the new Japanese ambassador to France, at 11 o'clock this morning and held a ceremony for presenting his credentials. Foreign Minister Poncet and civil and military officials from the presidential palace were in attendance. After the ceremony, Sato gave a speech, first saying that the friendly relations between France and Japan have lasted for a long time. Recently, France and Japan have been able to work together to seek the general happiness of mankind in all aspects. The Japanese ambassador then briefly outlined his past experience, saying that he was fortunate to be able to return to this capital with valuable friendships in Paris in the past, and he dared to assure the President that his purpose in serving here was to consolidate and develop the existing good relations between the two countries, and to further enhance this good relationship to the greatest extent possible, and to do his best to consolidate world peace. President Lebrun replied, first praising the achievements of the previous Japanese ambassador to France, and then saying that he was very pleased to see His Excellency return to this country, because his country has always been highly respectful of His Excellency. His Excellency came to his country the other day and worked hard for peace and international cooperation. His ambition, courage, and perseverance will never be forgotten by the people of his country. Now that His Excellency has returned to this land, he will be able to make France and Japan more united, and will receive the most sincere support from his government. (Havas, 28th)

British Overseas Trade Department Strongly Advocates Sino-British Cooperation

Seeking to promote British goods in the Chinese market

British newspapers praise our fulfillment of obligations

(London) The Overseas Trade Department today released a report on trade conditions from 1931 to 1933, strongly advocating that Chinese and British merchants cooperate in China to develop manufacturing, saying that if sufficient security can be obtained and a larger market for British goods is to be opened up in China, there is a fundamental principle that must be recognized, namely, that cooperation with Chinese merchants is necessary. The success of Japanese manufacturing may be matched by China in the future, which is very achievable. China's domestic cotton production is increasing day by day. Last year's imports of cotton goods were only 42 percent of the total in 1929. Therefore, it is expected that the imported goods will become less and less hot goods and more and more machinery and equipment. The United Kingdom can make up for its losses in cooked goods with machinery and other items. Today, the Chinese government is determined to appease the whole country and complete its construction work, which is an indelible sign. The Morning Post today published an article praising the efforts of the Chinese authorities to fulfill their obligations, saying that this example is worthy of emulation by borrowing countries that have a better reputation than China. (Reuters, 28th)

Britain and France Prepare to Start Negotiations to Avoid Economic War

(London) The Anglo-French economic war is expected to be avoided. According to today's news, the governments of the two countries have agreed to start talks as soon as possible to sort out their business relations. France has now decided to abolish the 15 percent surtax levied on British goods and has submitted a proposal to Congress to reduce the sales tax to 2 percent. The French government has notified the British government that it will strive to achieve its goals, so the talks between the two countries will definitely proceed smoothly in the future. (Reuters, 27th)

India's Increased Tariffs Cause Great Panic Among Japanese Merchants

Requesting government to fight for it

(Tokyo) All Japanese people are actively opposing India's new tariff system, believing that it has the nature of prohibiting the import of foreign goods. The government has received petitions from all parties requesting that the New Delhi meeting not continue. The government has also expressed great surprise at this matter, as the new tariffs also apply to goods that have already been shipped. Today, the Kobe Chamber of Commerce passed a resolution requesting the government to recall the Japanese representative in New Delhi and stop the progress of the Japanese-Indian meeting. The textile industry also petitioned the authorities to suspend the Japanese-Indian negotiations. It is said that unless the Indian side agrees not to increase tariffs on various goods, they can recognize the conditions of the Japanese concessions in the New Delhi meeting. At the same time, merchants in Kobe and Osaka have sent examples of the new Indian tax regulations to the government. According to reports, the new tax regulations increase the tax on tea sets by 550 percent, and the tax regulations for woven fabrics increase by 50 to 230 percent. According to Abe, chairman of the Osaka Cotton Transportation Federation, even if the government still insists on temporary forbearance, the Japanese delegation attending the New Delhi meeting will soon withdraw. (Reuters, 28th)

(Tokyo) According to reliable sources, the Japanese government has decided to order the Japanese delegation in New Delhi to apply to the Indian government to temporarily suspend the implementation of the new tax rules while negotiating an amicable solution. (Reuters, 28th)

Funeral of Car Crash Victims, a Sad Scene in Laon

(Paris) Today is the day of the funeral for the victims of the train accident in Laon. The coffins of the deceased were transported from the East Station. President Lebrun and government officials all came to participate. The crowds on the roadside were extremely crowded, all showing sadness. Lemaire, chairman of the East Road Railway Company, and Paganon, Minister of Public Works, delivered speeches one after another. President Lebrun bowed and paid his respects to the spirits. The Presidential Guard played mourning music, and sobs were heard from the crowd from time to time. (Havas, 27th)

Responsibility lies with the authorities to learn from the past and prevent future occurrences (Paris) The number of victims of the Laon train accident has reached 203, causing public unrest. There is now a demand that the authorities immediately find ways to prevent the recurrence of such tragedies and replace wooden trains with steel ones. It is heard that the government will submit emergency legislation regarding this case within days. The scene at the memorial service in East Garonne today was very moving. When Lemaire, director of the East Railway Bureau, gave his condolences, the relatives of the victims could not restrain their emotions and were all sobbing. Minister of Public Works Paganon, on behalf of the government, declared that he intended to investigate the case impartially. Today, Paganon issued a statement saying that France is willing to use its scientific strength to seek safety for the public. (Reuters, 27th)

Britain Learns a Good Lesson (London) In this French Laon train accident, all the dead were in wooden trains, while the steel trains were hardly damaged. The British public views this as a good lesson. After the French train accident, Britain immediately began an investigation and learned that only a small portion of the 63,000 trains in Britain were made of steel. One investigator even said that there were only 1,000 steel trains. It is expected that when Congress reconvenes in the future, it will discuss the issue of forcing railway companies to switch to steel trains. (Reuters, 27th)

Death and Mourning of the President of the Province of Spain

The Pan-American Conference Cooperates with the League of Nations

Avenol expresses comfort

Truce in Chaco extended to January 14

Bolivian government accepts Paraguay's dissent

(Geneva) The League of Nations regards the recognition and cooperation given to the League of Nations by the Pan American Union meeting in Montevideo as extremely important, as the relationship between the two organizations has been very cold in the past. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol issued a press release today expressing his comfort. The statement mentioned that US Secretary of State Hull submitted a resolution at the meeting warning Paraguay and Bolivia that since they are member states of the League of Nations, they should abide by the League of Nations Covenant and accept the handling procedures of the League of Nations Investigative Committee. He added that the conference's move greatly helped the committee's work to restore peace. It is heard that the committee is now seeking to extend the truce between the two countries until midnight on January 14 next year. (Reuters, 28th)

Capital of Uruguay Bolivia and Paraguay agreed to implement a truce from midnight on December 19 to midnight on December 30. Now the Bolivian government has accepted the proposal of the League of Nations Investigation Team and agreed to extend the deadline to January 14 next year. The Paraguayan representative issued a declaration saying that the only thing the government of that country expects is a fair resolution of the Gran Chaco incident, and that Paraguay's dignity, security, and rights should also be taken into account. (Havas, 28th)

Fire in Tokyo's Ginza

Modern men and women are frightened

(Tokyo) The Ginza Hall, a famous cafe in Tokyo, caught fire on the upper floor at 9 o'clock last night. 300 drunken customers and 150 waitresses fled in all directions, causing great chaos. The hall was eventually completely burned down, but fortunately no people or animals were injured. The cause was related to electrical leakage. (Telecommunication, 28th)

Closing of the Asian Student Congress

Resolution to Establish a European Federation of Eastern Students in the Capital of Italy

The Pope Grants an Audience to All Representatives

The University of Rome Hosts a Reception

Rome: At the final meeting of the Asian Student Congress held here today, a resolution was passed to establish a cultural center in Rome for students from the East and Far East, to be named the European Federation of Eastern Students. According to reports, this congress was attended by representatives of Asian students from over 500 European universities, having met here for a week and concluding today. (National Telegram, 28th)

Rome, Papal Capital: Over six hundred university students participating in the Asian University Students Congress were granted an audience by the Pope today, who delivered a brief speech, saying he was "extremely concerned about the great Asia" and was very pleased to meet with Asian youth. He also mentioned that the students had visited the Propaganda College, which he said was essentially owned by them all, and then gave each student his blessing. (Havas Dispatch)

Rome: The Asian Student Congress, held here, has now concluded. The University of Rome hosted a reception where representatives from various countries delivered speeches expressing their gratitude for the warm hospitality. The chairman of the Congress announced the intention to establish a "Permanent International Association of Students from the Near East, Middle East, and Far East." The Asian students were then received by the Undersecretary of the Italian Ministry of Corporations, Mr. Lusano, who gave a speech on the current state of the Italian corporatist system, stating that the "super-capitalism" adopted by Italy is a form of internationalism. He further stated, "It is not true culture to regulate the relationship between humans and machines. Only by regulating the relationship between humans with wisdom and justice can we call it true culture. Fascists are revolutionaries, and industrialists cannot consider themselves conservatives, because industrialists must use machines, and machines have a revolutionary nature. If industrialists are conservative, they will inevitably conflict with the machines they use. Those who destroy property are not revolutionaries. What we should abolish is ignorance and poverty." In conclusion, addressing the Asian students specifically, he said, "You are young and promising, and the responsibility for creating a new history for humanity rests on you. But since you bear the responsibility of creating history, you must first know what you desire is achievable. As for what we Italians desire, it is to work with the people of all countries with good intentions, friendship, and harmony to create a more just and humane social order." (Havas Dispatch, 28th)

US Actively Expanding Navy

Navy Department to Submit Proposal to Congress

To Seize Hegemony in the Pacific Ocean

(Washington) The US Navy Department disclosed today that it will request the next Congress to (1) authorize the President to maintain the Navy to the limits permitted by the treaties, and to replace warships that are too old when necessary; (2) In addition, it will also request a new shipbuilding fund of 100 million yuan in the 1934 naval budget to build two large destroyers, twelve light destroyers, six submarines, and to fund the construction expenses required for one battlecruiser and two light cruisers approved by the previous Congress; (3) It also intends to request Congress to increase the number of naval personnel from 79,500 to 82,500 next year. According to the US Navy's plan, it now intends to build 102 new ships at a cost of 560 million yuan by 1939, so that the US Navy can be equal to the British Navy, and in terms of quantity, exceed Japan according to the 5:5:3 ratio of the London Treaty. Building 32 ships using public works funds this year and 5 ships using the Navy's regular expenses is the first step in its shipbuilding program, and building 20 ships next year is the second step. According to people in the Navy Department, the shipbuilding program at this time will first pay attention to destroyers, submarines, and aircraft carriers, because they are the most urgently needed at present. If Congress can pass this proposal, the number of new ships built by the United States each year can be reduced to 13 in 1953. According to people in the Navy Department, the United States must now build one aircraft carrier, one heavy cruiser, five light cruisers, sixty-five destroyers, and thirty submarines to reach the strength permitted by the Washington Naval Treaty. Conversely, Japan has already built the full amount, and the United Kingdom is only 61 ships short of the strength permitted by the treaty. (National Telegram, 27th)

Rapid Advancement of Japanese Iron and Steel Industry

Many New Factories Established

Subsidized by the Japanese Government

(Paris) The Economic and Financial News Agency released a message yesterday stating, "The competition in the Japanese iron and steel industry is expanding day by day. The producers of iron are both subsidized by the Japanese government and benefited by the depreciation of the Japanese yen, and are not bound by the value set by the International Steel Industry Joint Management Company, so its export volume can increase by 50%. In addition, a new factory for steel cloth and two factories for manufacturing galvanized iron have just been established, and other factories for steel sheets, commercial steel, and steel ingots will also start operations within the second half of 1934. In addition to a new factory for steel pipes and a steelmaking plant, which are under construction, the Japanese also plan to establish steelmaking plants in China and Manchuria." (Havas Dispatch, 28th)

Roosevelt Hosts Banquet for Philippine Independence Delegation

Instructs Quezon to Prepare a Memorandum

Willing to Give Careful Consideration

(Washington) A White House spokesman announced today that President Roosevelt has ordered Philippine Senate President Quezon to submit a concrete proposal for resolving the Philippine independence issue. This matter was instructed during a banquet held at the White House yesterday for Quezon and other members of the independence delegation. However, the President does not bear any other responsibility other than guaranteeing that the submitted proposal will be given careful consideration. According to members of the independence delegation, Quezon is currently preparing a memorandum within one week. His proposal generally requests that the United States allow the Philippines to be independent in the near future based on economic conditions that are more favorable to the Filipinos than the original Philippine Independence Act. During yesterday's banquet, Quezon took the opportunity to present to the President that the sugar agreement rejected by Agriculture Secretary Wallace some time ago would greatly help the Philippines' finances, and requested that the President visit Manila after touring Puerto Rico and Hawaii in the future. US Mint Receives Silver to Mint Coins

Canadian Mining Resurrects Vitality

(Washington) The US National Government Mint announced today that it is ready to receive silver and mint silver coins in accordance with the proclamation issued by the President. (National Telegram, 27th)

Ottawa: Canadian silver mines produced 26 million ounces of silver in 1930. However, due to the sluggish silver price, production gradually decreased, and only 18 million ounces were produced in 1932. Now that US President Roosevelt has a policy of raising the silver price, and Canada also has the hope of ratifying the London Silver Agreement during this session of Congress, it is expected that Canadian silver mines will resume their activities. There are already important arrangements for preparing to mine silver on the east coast of Great Slave Lake. London financiers believe that President Roosevelt's silver policy will create a surplus of silver production, unless another method is found. The way to remedy this seems to be to implement the bimetallic system advocated by American silver-producing countries, or to restore the pre-war fineness of European silver coins. (Reuters Telegram, 27th)

Restoration Program Still Requires Expenses

Roosevelt Does Not Find It Strange

(Washington) The amount of the US budget deficit this year has exceeded 100 million yuan today, but it is still more than one-third lower than the 1,594,000,000 yuan deficit at the same time last year. President Roosevelt did not find this report strange, and said that the amount of the deficit may be more than this, because the later restoration program still requires expenses. President Roosevelt convened his advisors today to prepare the budget, and at the same time, the Ministry of Commerce reported that the foreign trade surplus in November was 56 million yuan. Cumming, the General Manager of the Deposit Insurance Corporation, stated today that the temporary guarantee fund that will begin next week can fully guarantee 97% of bank deposits, and the amount of insurance is limited to a maximum of 2,500 yuan per household. This is the most constructive way to protect deposits in banks. (Reuters Telegram, 28th)

Li Yangjing Inspects the Border Between Guangdong, Fujian, and Jiangxi

Li is Responsible for the Defense of the Fujian-Jiangxi Border

Huge Defensive Works Have Been Completed

Shantou correspondence: Li Yangjing, the commander of the 3rd Army of Guangdong, toured the East River this month. On the 4th, he convened a military conference at the Meixian military headquarters. Huang Renhuan, commander of the Independent 1st Division, Huang Yanzhen of the 7th Division, Huang Zhiwen of the 8th Division, Ouyang Xin, chief of staff of the 3rd Army, Yang Youmin, chief of staff of the Eastern District Command, Li Hua, director of the Highway Department, and Lu Zuoxin, director of the station, were all present. After the meeting, Li and Huang Renhuan went to Jiaoling to inspect the trenches along the Wuping border area. On the 11th, he and Ouyang Xin went from Jiaoling to Pingyuan. On the 13th, he arrived at Liuche, at the junction of Xunping, and immediately entered Xunwu, Chengjiang, and Jitan in Jiangxi to inspect the front line. In Xunwu City, he summoned the troops of the 8th Division to give a speech, roughly stating that the People's Government is now organizing in Fujian, and the Communist bandits in the border area between Fujian and Jiangxi are taking the opportunity to operate. The Red disaster has a tendency to rise again. Our army is responsible for the defense of Eastern Guangdong and should be on strict alert to maintain security. The current border deployment has been consolidated and there is no other danger in the area. The people in various sectors have been helping the government build roads and dig trenches, which is admirable. There is no need to suspect anything else. Our army vows to do its best to protect the territory and keep the people safe, so that all sectors can live and work in peace and the financial situation will not be adversely affected. On the 16th, Li returned to the Meixian military headquarters by car. The commanders of the 7th and 8th divisions went to Xingning to inspect the defenses. Xingning is currently guarded by Li Zhenliang's division. The two division commanders also went to Fengshun from Xingning to inspect the city defenses, because the city's huge defensive works have been completed and are used for the storage of firearms, ammunition, and food. There are four new trenches outside the city. On the 17th, Li inspected Dabu and the Chaozhou area via the Mei-Song road. He is expected to arrive in Shantou in about a day. Currently, Zhang Ruigui's division is responsible for the Chaozhou area, and Li is responsible for the Fujian-Jiangxi border. Li's visit to Shantou is to inspect the affairs of the Eastern District Pacification Commissioner's Office. The local areas of the counties on the Fujian border are becoming increasingly chaotic, and many people are fleeing into Guangdong territory. (22nd)

Hubei Army Encirclement and Suppression of Bandit Gangs in Southern Hubei

—Navy and Air Force Mobilized in Concert—

Wuchang Correspondence: The counties of Tongcheng, Chongyang, Tongshan, Yangxin, and Xianning in Southern Hubei have been plunged into a state of terror since the bandits from Jiangxi invaded. The bandits are the false 16th and 17th Armies, and have begun to take active action since the 20th. The false 17th Army is attacking Jinniu Town in Echeng County, and the false 16th Army is advancing towards Yangludong near Puchi in the south. The false 3rd and 7th Divisions are occupying Datian Mountain in Echeng and Yangxin, using it as a lair. Jinniu Town is only 120 miles from Wuchang and is an important location in southern Hubei. Yangludong also controls the hub of the Xiang-E Road. The authorities attach great importance to these two locations and have sent reinforcements, who will join forces to launch a major suppression campaign immediately. Zeng Yiding, commander of the Second Fleet, also boarded a warship from Hankou and went west along the Yangtze River to consolidate the river defenses. The task of protecting the Xiang-E Road, north of Puchi, is undertaken by Feng Xingxian's troops, and south of Linxiang, it is undertaken by Li Jue's division of the Hunan Army. There are also the 6th Railway Artillery Team and armored vehicles patrolling back and forth, which should be sufficient to ensure safety. According to foreign estimates, the bandits currently have no intention of attacking Wuhan. Their targets are no more than the following two routes: (1) Break through the Yangtze River bank and go to Xindi or Luoshan to enter Honghu; (2) Cross the river from Bailuoji and drive straight into Wufeng and Hefeng in Western Hubei, and join forces with the He bandits. However, the national army has a tight defense and their attempts will definitely be difficult to realize. (27th)

Red Bandits in the Border Area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces Almost Completely Eliminated

Bandit Leader Wu Huanxian's Whereabouts Unknown

Thorough Follow-Up is Urgently Needed

Kaifeng correspondence: The red bandits in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces were completely defeated by the national army in October. The remnants initially fled from Huang'an and Jingfu to the east, then to Shangcheng and Lihuang. Then, some of them returned to harass Huang'an and Jingfu. The commander was Wu Huanxian, commander of the false 25th Army (Wu is from Zhengjiabian in Jingfu, with 3,000 shi of rice at home, a graduate of the Wuhan Military and Political School, and the leader of the Huang'an faction among the false red bandits). Some retreated to poor valleys, relying on their location for self-preservation. A month ago, taking advantage of the troop deployments, the Communist bandits suddenly occupied Huangbeizhan, which belonged to Huang'an County, and were soon defeated. They fled north to the Dai Shiying and Zheng Bi Gao area. On the 10th of this month, they suddenly arrived at Daijia Village, a few miles from Jingfu City. The security squadron stationed there was completely sacrificed due to the disparity in numbers. The whereabouts of the captain Xu is unknown, and the two platoon leaders were abducted by the bandits. Liang Guanying, the commander-in-chief of the 25th Route Army, upon hearing the alarm, flew in reinforcements and captured a large number of people and guns. The bandits then retreated to Pengjia Dawang, 30 miles southeast of Jingfu, and held the dangerous pass to the death. After another four or five days of fierce fighting, they looted the cotton clothes and food of the refugees along Baishi'an and retreated to Yangsizhai. After another fierce attack, they collapsed in all directions. Wu's bandits' whereabouts are unknown. The bandit suppression headquarters in the border area is now offering a reward for his arrest. In Lihuang, which was originally the defense area of the 12th Division, the division was ordered to relocate on the 4th of this month, and the Zheng Regiment of Liang Guanying's troops took over. The red bandits hiding in the deep mountains then crept to the river bank two miles from the city and attacked the city with gunfire, creating an extremely critical situation. Fortunately, the Zheng Regiment calmly came out of the city to fight back, and the 54th Division of Hao Mengling's troops and the 64th Division of Wu Tinglin's Brigade flew to their aid and attacked the bandits' rear. On the 18th, they occupied Xuanjianshan and Daijiahe, and the bandits fled towards the Shi River. The leader of this group was Zhang, the chairman of the false Southeast Henan Soviet, who gathered 1,000 remnants of the false 82nd and 84th Divisions. After being severely wounded, the losses were almost complete. Currently, the indigenous bandits have all been pacified, but it is impossible for the foreign bandits to escape privately. Those who are to be pacified lack guarantors and have no choice but to put their lives at risk. However, the number is limited, so the bandits' power has been greatly reduced. The former nest of the bandits, Chengmagang in Macheng, has a people's defense team stationed there and is as peaceful as ever. There is no trace of bandits. In the Huang'an and Lishan areas, there are only small groups of kidnappers, which is not a cause for concern. However, there are no less than 30,000 guns hidden in the border area, and the refugees have no clothes or food. If remittances are sent, there is no grain available for purchase locally. If grain is transported, the mountain roads are rugged and difficult to travel. Liu Zhenju now plans to send the refugees to Liu'an, Huoqiu, Qianshan, Taihe, and Hefei for temporary food relief. If the follow-up is not thorough, it is absolutely impossible to avoid a resurgence. (26th)

Inspection Tour of Gan, Anhui, Xiang, and Hubei (Special Correspondent for this Newspaper, Ren An)

General Situation of Liu'an Governance After the Disaster

Past Redification Full of Scars

Liu'an Correspondence: Western Anhui has always been known for its richness, bordering Henan and Hubei, with abundant mountains, bamboo, and wood, especially rich in tea and hemp. However, due to traffic congestion, exports are difficult, and a large amount of goods are stored. Not only has its material potential not been fully realized, but the import of politics and culture is also difficult. The people's nature, if not frivolous, is lazy. In the past, officials and gentry used high-pressure tactics to exploit arbitrarily, and arrogant and cunning people incited and bewitched them, leading to deep public resentment, which was seized by the Red Bandits, resulting in the great disaster of Western Anhui. In recent years, the National Army has achieved great victories in encirclement and suppression. The urban and rural towns along the Pi River have been recovered. The Red Bandit pseudo-armies 25 and 28 on the west bank of the Shi River have also been defeated one by one, and most of them have been annihilated. A small number of the remaining bandits, three to five hundred, have fled into the deep mountains and valleys to survive. However, with intensified blockades, they are increasingly lacking oil, salt, and food. If they do not surrender and rehabilitate, they will also perish on their own.

Since taking office, Qin Zhenfu, the Administrative Inspector of the Third District and concurrently the Magistrate of Liu'an County, has made great efforts to promote the pacification of refugees, the protection of the locality, the construction of roads, the increase in production, the implementation of compulsory education, and the exposure of local tyrants and evil gentry. According to local sources, although it has been more than a year since the National Army recovered the counties in the district ravaged by the Red Bandits, the clearing of scattered bandits, the elimination of heresies, the handling of aftermath, the restoration of rural areas, and the newly promulgated important policies such as autonomy, self-defense, and construction have not yet fundamentally taken effect. The reason for this is that the people do not understand the government's administrative methods and have not been able to cooperate in the implementation. Now, the government has established a propaganda section to formulate a propaganda outline and various propaganda materials, which are sent to various counties in groups to go deep into the countryside to explain the methods of implementing new policies, to inform about the need to cooperate in suppressing bandits, and to examine the administrative situation of each county, the suffering of the people, and the urgent needs of the locality, so that nothing can be ordered to each county to be implemented quickly.

When Commissioner Qin Zhenfu first arrived in Liu'an last year, he saw citizens inside and outside the city enjoying the cool in the evening, mostly using cool beds and smoking opium in the streets. After strict prohibition, they gradually disappeared. Opium dens and opium donations were used to fund the Public Security Bureau and the detective team. This July, it was also changed to be borne by the commercial firms. The opium dens were sealed, and the opium equipment was burned. The police and bailiffs, who used to number over a hundred, were mostly unpaid and relied entirely on issuing tickets and collecting extra money. Each ticket was at least ten yuan or more, and extortion was even worse in criminal cases. Now, they have been thoroughly reorganized, and the number of people has been reduced by more than half. The monthly expenses, in addition to the collection of entertainment donations and commercial firm donations, are said to be still less than three hundred yuan. In the officialdom, there are still old titles such as "Your Excellency," "Master," and "Advisor," which carry the stench of the autocratic political system of feudal society. The commissioner has also ordered their abolition.

After the county was recovered, in terms of facilities, more than 100 rural cooperative preparatory societies have been established to relieve rural finance, with loans of more than 39,000 yuan to purchase seeds and plowing cattle to relieve the spring famine. Education is handled in accordance with the outline of educational facilities for the people in the recovered bandit areas, unifying the income and expenditure of educational funds, abolishing the double landlords of school fields, and stipulating the restoration methods of various schools, such as organizing short-term primary schools, investigating out-of-school children, improving private schools, promoting ancestral halls, setting up private schools in guild halls, setting up people's education halls in schools in urban and suburban areas, and especially running teacher training courses to widely train teachers to promote education. Farmers in each village have organizations such as the militia team and the anti-communist volunteer team to take on the responsibility of investigating bandits and protecting public security. The only requirement of the farmers at present is to hope that the scattered bandits will be cleared, the taxes will be reduced, so that they can live and work in peace and contentment.

The Rural Financial Relief Office of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei and Anhui has established a county branch in Liu'an, established a rural cooperative preparatory society, and implemented loans. According to the method, farmers in the newly recovered areas who are over 20 years old, have independent living qualifications, and can gather nine people to form a group, and submit it to the county branch for approval, may establish a rural cooperative preparatory society, and borrow money for proper purposes according to the prescribed procedures. After one year, the preparatory society may be changed to a formal "rural credit cooperative". This year, all members of the preparatory society borrow money from the preparatory society, the annual interest rate is one cent. When the preparatory society borrows from the county branch, the annual interest rate is eight li. Each member is jointly and severally liable for the repayment of the debt. Currently, 112 preparatory societies have been established in Liu'an County, with a total of 5,065 members and a total loan amount of 39.490 yuan. Each person averages over seven yuan. The categories of funds used are eight items such as purchasing seeds, food, feed, fertilizer, farm tools, livestock, repairing houses, and others. The largest percentage is the purchase of food, accounting for a little less than 38% of the total, followed by seeds accounting for a little less than 17%, and repairing houses accounting for a little more than 13%.

According to the eyewitness accounts of the county government and local people about the situation during the Red Bandit occupation in the past, most of the title deeds of farmland have been destroyed. Because Liu'an is a county close to the mountains, the fields are uneven in height, so it is impossible to merge them, and they remain as they were. Farming has not been abandoned at all. However, tea mountains and bamboos and trees in the southwest have been cut down a lot. Due to the impact of the blockade, the hemp producing area has no sales market, and the output has been greatly reduced. Many houses in the war traffic zone have been burned. The houses of public offices and wealthy gentry are mostly used as county, district and township Soviet governments. Among the farmers who died, the largest number were those who were gray in attitude, were attacked by both sides, and were forced to serve as bandits and died in battle. Land was distributed in units of villages, and three dou of land per person was the standard. Each dou of land could harvest more than two shi of grain. However, it was limited to small and medium-sized workers and farmers. After the wealthy farmers' properties were confiscated, they could only get barren land. After the land was distributed, work also followed, such as being a detective, guarding, digging trenches, washing clothes, sewing, touching melons (killing people), etc., and there were economic obligations to pay various progressive taxes. Even if there was a surplus after the income and expenditure were equal, it was not much, and they were not allowed to buy or sell or hire people to cultivate. If they were Red Bandits or engaged in pseudo-government work, a substitute farming team would be formed to cultivate for them. If there was a surplus after the distribution, it would be allocated to the public and operated by the substitute farming team. Cash and women's jewelry were absorbed and recast into silver coins, which the people were forced to use. There was also the Pseudo-Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Border Province Soviet Farmers Bank, which indiscriminately issued paper money. Although pseudo-cooperatives tried hard to steal and sell bamboo, wood, tea, hemp, and other items outside the bandit area, they could not do it due to the strict blockade. Prices gradually fell, and finance became increasingly depleted, which can be imagined. Lenin Primary Schools were set up in various villages to promote redification, and personnel were sent by the Pseudo-Soviet government to teach without special funding, which was easy to promote. If there were mutual attacks or secret accusations, a general meeting of the whole township would be called to make a public decision. In addition to ordinary crimes, they would be punished with corvée and imprisonment. If they were convicted of being reactionary, they would be immediately brutally killed. Even the closest relatives were not allowed to have any pity. In total, the number of farmers who joined the bandits was about 15,000, mostly poor farmers, hired farmers, and craftsmen. Among the craftsmen, barbers were the most. After the recovery, about 12,000 people surrendered themselves, mostly the old, weak, and young. Most of the able-bodied men were forced to serve as bandits or engaged in pseudo-Soviet government work, and died in the repeated encirclement and suppression wars or in the bandits' mutual killings (such as exposing AB groups, reorganization factions, and using terrorist policies to suppress rebellious elements). Only a very limited number of people are still fleeing elsewhere.

As for the method of handling the recovered land, it is based on Articles 13 and 15 of the Regulations on Land Handling in Bandit Suppression Areas promulgated by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Three Provinces. The county government announces registration, and the owners receive management certificates, restore the original land rights according to the original boundaries of the land, and cultivate their own land. Those who have done important work during the banditization, or are quick-witted, especially literate youths, are transferred to the reformatories run by the government to receive special education. They graduate in March and return to their hometowns.

Songjiang

Suspicious Person Found in Inn

Xu Jinsheng from Fengjing was lodging at the Xie Sheng Inn last night when he was encountered by a police inspection. At that time, Xu Jinsheng was holding banknotes in his hand and looked flustered. When questioned, he claimed to be a painter in a lacquer shop on Foch Road in Shanghai, and came to Songjiang to open a lacquer shop, and then claimed to be traveling. His words were contradictory. When asked about the amount of banknotes, he stared blankly and did not know the number. Therefore, an inspection was carried out, and a leather suitcase and rattan suitcase were found, with a camel's hair robe and 71 yuan in silver inside the suitcase. He also claimed that he would go to Pudong, then Songjiang was not a necessary place to pass, which was quite suspicious. Fearing that it was related to a theft case, Xu Jinsheng, the banknotes, suitcases, etc. were sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Suzhou

A Minor Quarrel Leads to Murder

Li Dai, a young woman at No. 32 Guan Alley, Sibaidu, outside Changmen, quarreled with her neighbor Pan Li a few nights ago over a minor matter. The next day, Li Dai suddenly swallowed opium and still went to Pan Li's house to talk. At that time, Pan Li saw that her expression had changed, asked about the situation, and immediately sent her to Gengsheng Hospital for treatment. However, due to excessive poisoning, she died at 10 pm. The police station in charge sent Pan Li to the station for interrogation, and at the same time reported to the District Procuratorate to send someone to inspect.

Famous Lawyer Accused of Libel

Lu Hongyi, a famous lawyer in Suzhou, pointed out two weeks ago at a banquet hosted by Lin Biao, the President of the High Court, for the Minister of Justice, that the Judicial Investigation Committee had committed dereliction of duty and malpractice. The next day, President Lin suspended Zhu Zhongqi, a member of the Judicial Investigation Committee. Zhu believed that Lu Hongyi deliberately set out to damage the reputation of others, so he filed a self-complaint with the Wuxian District Court on the charge of libel. After the court accepted the case, it scheduled a hearing on January 10. At that time, there will be a grand debate between the two parties.

Wuxi

Apprentice Murders Master

Tang Minggen, a villager in Yangming Township, Beiqiao Street, Third District of the county bureau, 38 years old, opened a bamboo shop in the street. There was one customer master in the shop, named Shen Rongbo, and three apprentices. The eldest apprentice was named Ji Chulin, 19 years old, from Yangzhou. On the 25th of this month, Ji returned to his hometown from Ximen in the city and brought back eight glutinous rice balls. He asked Tang Minggen if he was hungry. Tang ate three of them because he had not eaten dinner. When he ate the fourth one, he took a bite and suddenly felt that the taste was different, so he immediately threw it to the ground. At that time, his youngest apprentice, Wang Mingzhuang, was holding one next to him, also took a bite, felt a different taste, and threw it away. Unexpectedly, after a short while, both of them felt upset and vomited non-stop. By midnight, customer master Shen Rongbo returned. Tang told him what had happened, and knew that there was something wrong. He repeatedly questioned Ji, and finally got the truth. Ji said that he had used the excuse of using medicine for sores in Ximen and bought arsenic at a certain drugstore, mixed it into the glutinous rice balls, and lied to the master to eat it, in order to murder him, etc. After hearing this, Shen immediately used egg white salt soup to irrigate the two of them. Wang Mingzhuang has recovered because of the lighter poisoning. Tang Minggen is still out of danger, in a coma. After this incident happened, the First Resident Office of the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge arrested Ji Chulin that night. According to the confession, the poisoning was instigated by Tang Minggen's brother, Mingda. The office sent a police officer to summon Tang Mingda. Because Mingda was also seriously ill in bed, he could not be brought to justice. Someone temporarily guaranteed him. Ji Chulin was temporarily detained in the bureau. Tang Minggen sent someone to Yangzhou to invite his father to Wuxi to negotiate.

Changzhou

Wage Dispute Resolved at Qingfeng Factory

Workers from the Qingfeng Silk Factory in Wuxi came to Changzhou to ask Wanfengtai Tobacco Shop for their wages. The matter was delayed for two days and could not be resolved. On the morning of the 27th, the party and government organs made a final mediation and decided that Yao, Juncheng, a friend of Wanfengtai, would advance 1,700 yuan, and the mediation organs would advance 800 yuan, totaling 2,500 yuan, which would be sent to the county government. Yan Zhichen, the assistant manager of the Qingfeng Silk Factory, came to the county to receive the money. The factory will be responsible for raising and distributing another 1,800 yuan and dismissing the workers in the factory. All account books and ledgers of the Qingfeng Factory are limited to the responsibility of Hui and Yan to be handed over to the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce within three days for regular liquidation. The workers' representatives were satisfied. At about 6 pm, Hui and Yan arrived at the county and received the 2,500 yuan of workers' wages. At about 8 pm, they led the workers back to Wuxi by car.

Detective Team Arrests Notorious Bandit from Cheng County

Zhou Peida, a notorious bandit from Jiangyin, is from Qiuzhuang in the county. He is an accomplice of Yang Yaoda and Gao Xiaosheng, notorious bandits who have been executed. He has been wanted for a long time but has not been captured. The bandit sneaked into Changzhou on the 27th and hid in a toilet on the south bank of Huimin Bridge. The matter was detected by Ni Gusheng, the captain of the detective team, who led the team members to arrest him.

Changshu

Donglai Town Robbed by Bandits

Donglai Town, in the Fourth District of this county, has convenient transportation and a flourishing market. It is the leading town in the northwest of Changshu. The residents of the area are very simple and most of them are well-off. At about 7 pm on the night of the 27th of this month, suddenly 70 to 80 sea bandits came from the northeast riverbank, all armed with guns, and robbed the town. When they arrived in the town, they first confiscated all the guns and weapons of the patrol boats of the Third District Water Police stationed in the town, and cut off the telephone lines before starting the robbery. All households and shops were spared. The area has Shanghai branch-set-up Xin Xin, Zhen Xin and other yarn factories flower collection offices, and Shen Yantai rice mills, Shunfeng flower trade, suffered heavy losses. At the time of the robbery, traffic was cut off and order was disrupted. Fortunately, the mayor Fan Dongsheng urgently sent a special messenger to Lu Yuan Town (about six or seven li away) to report to various places by telephone. After the Xigang District Office and the Xitangqiao Public Security Bureau learned about it, it was already around 9:30. When the team was sent, the thieves had gone far away. The thieves also robbed when they passed through Black Star Port. According to statistics, the losses in the two towns are about tens of thousands of gold.

Yangzhou

Fairness Project Bridge Completed

The Gongdao Bridge in the northern township of Jiangdu is no less in length than the Wanfu Bridge in the eastern township. The bridge was completely washed away after the great flood in the autumn of the 20th year. For a time, traffic was blocked. Local gentry Wang Shaohe and others raised funds to rebuild it, and the bridge embankment was built with soil and trees were planted to consolidate the embankment. The project area lasted for two years, and it was recently completed, and traffic has been completely restored. Yesterday (26th), in order to prevent tree felling and damage to the embankment, the association publicly submitted the case to the Ninth District Office and forwarded it to the county government for announcement and protection.

Jiashan

President of Industrial Bank Robbed of Huge Sum of Money

Chen Zixiang, Vice President of Shanghai Zhejiang Industrial Bank, (from Xiaoshan, 31 years old) set off from Shanghai on the 20th of this month to collect debts from money houses in Nanxun and other places. After finishing, he transferred to Tangqi to Hangzhou. In the Dagou River area, he was robbed by bandits. It is estimated that he was robbed of more than 4,700 yuan in account money, as well as diamond rings and gold watches. In addition to reporting the robbery to the bureau in Hangzhou to pursue the bandits, President Chen set off overnight to the county and stayed at the Jiashan Hotel. As soon as the account money from Ganyao and other places in the county was collected, he went to Xingfu to report.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Zhuxiaowan

Meng Afa, a farmer in Zhuxiaowan, Xitang Township, lives by farming. He has only one son, 11 years old. A dozen bandits suddenly came the other night, wantonly robbed Meng's house, and kidnapped Meng's son. They also threatened that he must prepare a huge sum of money to get the ticket, otherwise his life would not be guaranteed. The Meng family heard the words and was extremely frightened.

Nanjing

Capital Film Inspection Committee Works Tensely

Since Li Jiaxiang took over as the Standing Committee Member of the Capital Film Inspection Committee, the handling of all committee affairs has been even more strict than before. At the beginning of his tenure, Li convened a meeting with all the inspection agents stationed in Beijing to inquire whether there were any difficulties or negligence on the part of the staff in the meeting, so that the staff could be ordered to reform to avoid difficulties for the agents. Recently, as the end of the year is approaching, the film companies have been very crowded to send their films to the committee for inspection. In order to take care of the film merchants, the committee inspects them day and night, inspecting about five feature films and ten short films every day. Moreover, after each day's inspection, those who are approved for screening, Li will personally urge the responsible staff to issue licenses on schedule, so the working hours of the staff in the committee are increased by two hours to seven sentences before they stop working. It is also heard that because the committee is required to take three days off for the New Year as usual, the films to be inspected on New Year's Eve, if approved for screening, will also be issued licenses within the year, so as not to be delayed in the committee for a long time.

Local News

The Chance of War in Fujian is Imminent

Fujian Redification Shops Closed

Air Force is Weak, Less Than Twenty Aircraft

Certain Army Advances, Foreigners Safely Relocated

Great War Within Ten Days - Shanghai Shishi News Agency: The situation on the Zhejiang-Fujian border has become quite tense in recent days. There have been occasional contacts on the front line. The Shishi News Agency reporter met a certain member of the Central Committee staying in Shanghai yesterday. According to the talk, according to recent news from a certain source, the Fujian side has decided to concentrate its efforts to fight the Central Army. Now, due to the terrain, there is no room for development in all directions, and the economy is tight and the military strength is weak. It is really impossible to conduct large-scale operations. Because the current operations of the Fujian side are purely defensive, there will never be a direct conflict for a while. As for the plan adopted, it is quite similar to that of the Red Bandits against the Central Army. Judging from the current situation, the main force of the Central Army's current operations is still the army and air force, which have been largely arranged. According to the observation of the current situation, the war is imminent, about no later than one week after New Year's Day. At that time, the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee will be opened, and the political situation will have a considerable impact on this.

Fujian Guests Talked About Redification - Ouyashe News Agency said: According to a certain gentleman from Fujian Province in Shanghai yesterday, a large number of fellow villagers from various parts of Fujian have fled to Shanghai recently. Every ship arriving in Shanghai is full of these people. What the newspaper reported yesterday that those who fled from Fujian Province to Shanghai were mostly to avoid the war. In fact, this is just a part of the reason. However, there are other reasons. Since the Fujian side has moved from a tacit military understanding with the Communist Party to a political fusion, the two sides have demarcated areas of defense and made a covenant of offensive and defensive alliance. Now Changting, Yongding, Longyan and other counties have been officially handed over to the Communist Army by the pseudo-government to be stationed and governed. The local wealth and upright gentry have fled and are completely in a state of redification. If the Central authorities do not actively suppress the Fujian rebellion, it is feared that Fujian Province will follow the example of the counties in the Jiangxi bandit area and become an irrecoverable situation.

Yanping Recovered Confirmed - Huadong News Agency said: Regarding the news that Yanping has been recovered by the Central Army, the Huadong News Agency reporter specifically inquired from the Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications in this city. According to the bureau, the commercial telegraph line from Shanghai to Yanping has been able to reach Yanping via Pucheng since yesterday. Therefore, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau has resumed receiving telegrams to Yanping as usual yesterday. This is a definite proof that Yanping has been recovered. In addition, the information received by the local authorities from the front said that the Central Army had indeed left the south side of Jian'ou a few days ago and arrived in Nanping. Nanping belongs to the first county of Yanping and is not far from Yanping. Therefore, it is indeed possible for the Central Army to reach Yanping.

Limit the Chamber of Commerce to Pay Huge Sum of Money - Xinxin News Agency said: According to the Fujian merchants in Shanghai who received a telegram from Xiamen yesterday, the telegram roughly stated that the Fujian government has been extremely financially strained since it announced its establishment. Now, in order to prepare for the invasion of Zhejiang, the military expenses required are very large. A special envoy has been sent to the Chamber of Commerce to declare that it is limited to paying 500,000 yuan immediately and must not delay military affairs. It is learned that most of the shops in Fuzhou, Zhangzhou and other cities have now unanimously closed and temporarily suspended business.

Fujian Air Force is Weak - Dabai News Agency said: The air force strength of the Fujian side is very weak. It is found that the Fujian side has planes, in addition to the four captured from the former reorganized Zhang Zhen troops, the four or five detained from the reorganized Chen Guohui troops, and the few owned by the Communist Party and the Social Democratic Party. In addition to the original several aircraft, 12 new aircraft were ordered from abroad, but only six have been shipped, totaling less than 20. Most of them are reconnaissance aircraft, and only two or three are bombers. Moreover, there is no aviation talent and no combat effectiveness, so the aircraft have been hidden in remote places.

Surrendered Army Has Advanced - Riri News Agency said: It has just been reported from a certain military agency in this city that after the 19th Route Army Independent Regiment surrendered to the Central Government, they supported Qian Yuguang as the regiment commander. The troops have established contact with the Central Army and have now crossed Pucheng and are advancing towards Nanya from Jian'ou. The vanguard battalion □ had a brief contact there last night. The other party is in an encircled situation, and there will be a fierce battle within a few days.

Foreigners Safely Relocated - Ouyashe News Agency said: According to news from the foreign community in this city, after the Central Government notified all foreigners to relocate to safe areas as soon as possible, the consuls of various countries in Fuzhou and other places immediately ordered them to relocate. Japanese citizens had already moved to Cangqianshan on the 24th, and other British, American and French nationals also evacuated one after another. When necessary, they will board the warships of their respective countries stationed in Fujian. Yesterday, Mr. Moriya, the Japanese Consul General in Fuzhou, sent a telegram to the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai to report the safety of the country's citizens.

Establishment of the Association of Fujian West Shanghai Groups to Save Hometown

The Association of Fujian West Shanghai Groups to Save Hometown was established at the Weiya Restaurant on Sima Road at 3 pm yesterday afternoon. More than ten representatives including Wu Yuwen and Su Qi attended the meeting. Wu Yuwen was elected chairman and Chen Huimin was the recorder. First, the chairman reported that Western Fujian is a densely populated and resource-rich area of Fujian. Since the Communist bandits occupied Changting and captured Yan Yong in the 20th year of the Republic of China, most of our fellow villagers have been displaced and have taken refuge in foreign lands. There are also tens of thousands in Shanghai alone. Although there were organizations of various township associations before, there was no overall contact. In order to concentrate the strength of the groups and seek the welfare of the homeland together, this association was specially organized. Then, the proposals were discussed and it was decided that (1) the declaration proposal will be handed over to the Executive Committee for handling, and (2) the amendment of the articles of association will be passed. Then, the executive committee was elected. As a result, Wu Yuwen, Su Qi, Lai Xueping, Chen Huimin, Fan Jianqiu, and others were elected as executive committee members. They had a dinner and dispersed.

Since Fujian formed its own government and separated from the Central Government, the news has been spread, and everyone has different opinions. Fuzhou Authorities Take Over the China Merchants Bureau Branch Office Buildings

Troops from the Anti-Smuggling Bureau Stationed There

Fuzhou News: The local government has dispatched personnel to take over the buildings of the Fujian branch of the state-run China Merchants Bureau and has stationed troops there. Details are as follows:

Anti-Smuggling Team Takes Over: At the beginning of the Fujian Incident, the People's Government did not take over the buildings of the Fuzhou branch of the China Merchants Bureau. Recently, the Anti-Smuggling Team of the Ministry of Finance of the People's Government, due to the lack of accommodation for its soldiers, sent personnel to investigate. The conclusion was that the China Merchants Bureau was a state-run organization and that its Fuzhou branch should be taken over for official use. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance first sent a representative to the bureau to explain the purpose to the director of the Fuzhou branch of the China Merchants Bureau and then dispatched troops to station there.

Public Security Bureau Inspects: At the same time, the Fuzhou Public Security Bureau sent Section Chief Lei Yulin, along with personnel from the Anti-Smuggling Team of the Ministry of Finance, to the branch office and ordered the director to vacate all the buildings in the bureau for the receiving personnel. Lei Yulin of the Public Security Bureau was also dispatched to the bureau to supervise the inspection. At that time, the personnel in the branch office did not dare to resist due to the pressure of force and had to agree to move out.

Troops Have Moved In: After the Anti-Smuggling Bureau of the Ministry of Finance took over, the soldiers of the Anti-Smuggling Bureau immediately moved into the bureau. It is now reported that all the buildings of the branch office have been occupied by the anti-smuggling soldiers, and the devastation is indescribable. It is also said that the warehouses of the branch office have not yet been occupied by the People's Government.

Encourage the Operation of Liners: The members of the receiving committee of the China Merchants Bureau's Fujian branch, such as Lei Yulin, did not take over the small steamships owned by the bureau when they took over the buildings. According to Lei and others, although the China Merchants Bureau is a state-run organization, the People's Government is actively protecting the traffic of commercial ships and will not allow accidents to happen. Why has your bureau's Fuzhou liners stopped sailing? You can continue to operate as usual. We guarantee that there will be no unexpected dangers.

Report to the Shanghai Head Office: After the branch office was taken over by the People's Government, the director of the Fujian branch has already found ways to move and store all the business accounts and official documents to avoid loss. At the same time, he has submitted a report to the general manager of the Shanghai head office, Liu Hongsheng, for verification. It is reported that the address and buildings of the branch office were previously mortgaged to a certain bank, and there is a creditor-debtor relationship. Now that they have been taken over by the Fujian authorities, a letter should be sent to the creditor to inform them.

Telephone Service in the City Center Officially Opened at 6:30 AM Yesterday

Telephone Bureau Allocates Fifteen Pairs of Cables for Municipal Government Use

Seven Pairs Directly Connected to the Concession, Eight Pairs Relay from Jiangwan Bureau

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, after the completion of the new municipal government building, with the municipal government and its subordinate bureaus moving in and starting to work one after another, in order to facilitate communication, specially started laying a cable of 50 pairs from the Zhabei Branch in the middle of last month, connecting to the city center area, and allocated 15 pairs for the municipal government and various bureaus to use. It is divided into seven pairs of concession cables, with the municipal government providing its own 200-line switchboard, directly connected to the concession, and eight pairs of Chinese area cables, which are temporarily relayed by the Jiangwan Branch before the establishment of the new bureau. The remaining 35 pairs are reserved for user installation. After the craftsmen were dispatched to actively install and test the calls in sections, and the sound waves were corrected, the official calls with the Chinese and Concession areas started at 6:30 AM yesterday.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the new municipal government telephones have been connected since yesterday. The numbers are "4121", "4122", "4123", "4124", "4125", "4126", "4127", "4128". To call from the concession, first dial "02" and have the concession central station relay the call. To call to the concession, dial "0" to connect.
