Sanbei's Shanghai-Jiang Liner Hongli Runs Aground in Jianli

Following the loss of Sanbei Company's Qingpu steamer, disasters continued with Wanxiang and Hengshan's collision. Now, the Yangtze River upstream liner Hongli has run aground in Jianli. Misfortunes have been accumulating. The situation is described in detail below.

Grounding in Jianli: Recently, the water level in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River has been receding very quickly. The water level at Chenglingji is only zero inches, making navigation very difficult. In the past week, the Changsha liners of various companies have been blocked in that area. This time, the Sanbei Company's Hongli steamer, sailing from Changsha, Hunan, back to Shanghai, ran aground on the Jianli River on the morning of the 27th of this month due to the sharp drop in the river water. When the Shashi Sanbei branch received the news, it immediately tried to send a ship to rescue it.

Hongzhen Damages Blades: Sanbei has four ships operating on the Hunan-Changsha route. After Hongli ran aground, the Shashi branch originally planned to send Hongzhen, which was on the upper river, to rescue it. Unexpectedly, Hongzhen's propeller blades were damaged and it could not sail to Jianli for a while. Therefore, another ship could only be sent to tow Hongli. The Shashi branch has telegraphed the Shanghai head office.

Hongheng Goes to Rescue: The company's Hongheng steamer is currently sailing upstream from downstream to Hunan. The Shashi branch has ordered the ship to sail to Jianli to try to tow Hongli out of the shallows. Rescue is currently underway. Details are still awaiting further reports. Also, the case of the company's Hengshan steamer colliding with and sinking a sand barge in Zhenjiang is being handled by the Zhenjiang Customs. The contents of this matter can only be fully understood after Hengshan returns to Shanghai and the shipowner is questioned. Hengshan, which ran aground on the riverbank in Nanjing, has been towed out and is now loading cargo and will be able to sail to Shanghai soon.

Ministry of Communications Orders China Merchants Bureau to Stop Hiring Foreign Seafarers

No Renewal of Employment After Expiration of Term

The Shanghai China Merchants Bureau recently received an instruction from the Ministry of Communications that the general manager's office of the China Merchants Bureau stop hiring foreign captains, and that foreign captains and crew members not be rehired after the expiration of their terms. Chinese crew members should be promoted according to their qualifications in order to safeguard navigation rights. The original text recorded by the Daily News reporter is as follows: "According to the China Merchant Seafarers' and Drivers' Association, 'When the China Merchants Bureau was first established, most of the crew members at all levels were foreigners. This was because Chinese people lacked nautical talents and had to borrow talents from foreign countries, resulting in the loss of sovereignty, which is deeply regrettable. Fortunately, in recent years, Chinese people have worked hard and are gradually becoming more proficient in nautical knowledge. Crew members at all levels in the bureau have begun to be filled by Chinese people. After the bureau was placed under the management of the National Government, the principle was that crew members at all levels would be filled by Chinese people, and vacant positions would be filled by promotion according to qualifications. Therefore, the number of Chinese people serving as crew members in the bureau has gradually increased, and there are also many Chinese people who have been promoted to captain. It is fortunate that nautical sovereignty is gradually being recovered, which is a glory for the country. Since Chinese people have served as captains, they have been careful and cautious, and their achievements have been excellent. In the past, when foreigners served as captains, accidents occurred frequently, such as the confiscation of the Xinhua, Xinji, Xinchang, and Xinkang steamers, which is clear evidence. Furthermore, according to the laws of various countries, for the sake of sovereignty, captains are mostly filled by their own nationals. Moreover, the high salaries of foreign captains are a waste of the national treasury, which is a minor matter. We have now heard that the bureau has the motivation to re-employ foreign captains, such as recently hiring a foreigner to serve as the captain of the Xinfeng steamer. This not only violates the inherent principle, but also fears that nautical sovereignty will be lost again. This is a matter of heartbreak. We do not know what General Manager Liu of the bureau is thinking, putting the country's navigation rights aside? The association, seeing this situation, cannot remain silent and hereby submits a report to your department, ordering the general manager that foreign captains who are in office not be re-employed after the expiration of their terms, and that when there is a vacancy for a captain, Chinese crew members should be promoted according to their qualifications, and no more foreigners should be hired, so as to safeguard navigation rights, which would be fortunate for the country.'" Based on this, in addition to the instructions, it is hereby ordered that the bureau investigate and submit its opinions for verification. This order."

Clerks of Two Radio Stations Strike Yesterday Due to Dissatisfaction with Treatment

Ministry of Communications Orders Immediate Return to Service

Removal and Dismissal for All Who Fail to Report by Deadline

The clerical staff of the International Radio Station and the Shanghai Wireless Telegraph Office, both under the Ministry of Communications, went on strike at 0:05 yesterday morning due to dissatisfaction with the treatment stipulated by the Ministry. The Ministry of Communications ordered the two stations to publish a notice in the newspapers, ordering all personnel to return to their posts by the deadline, otherwise they would be dismissed. The details are as follows:

Preferential Treatment for Radio Operators: The staff of the radio stations are divided into three departments: technical (i.e., engineers, etc.), telegraphic (i.e., sending telegrams, etc.), and clerical (i.e., receiving and sending telegrams, collecting payments, accounting, general affairs, etc.). The treatment for technicians is at least 70 yuan per month and at most 360 yuan. The treatment for telegraphers ranges from 32 yuan to 300 yuan. The treatment for clerical staff ranges from 32 yuan to 160 yuan. Those whose salaries are below 40 yuan will receive an increase of 3 yuan for each grade promotion. Those whose salaries are above 40 yuan will receive an increase of 4 yuan for each grade promotion. The maximum increase for each grade promotion is 10 yuan.

Performance Evaluation and Promotion: The Ministry of Communications recently promulgated the "Rules of Operation," which contains measures for performance evaluation and promotion. Performance evaluations are conducted every six months and are divided into three grades: excellent (3 points), good (2 points), and average (1 point). Those who have accumulated 6 points in performance evaluation will be promoted by one grade, which will increase their original salary. At the same time, it is stipulated that one-third of the total number of employees in each radio station can enjoy the excellent grade. Therefore, there must be two excellent grades each year in order to be promoted by one grade. If each performance evaluation is average, it will take three years to be promoted by one grade.

Requests for Improvement: Because the duties of the clerical staff are easier than those of the other two departments, they rarely enjoy the excellent grade in each performance evaluation and must take at least one and a half years to be promoted by one grade. The Ministry of Communications also subsidizes technicians 12 to 50 yuan per month, and telegraphers 8 to 35 yuan per month, but clerical staff receive nothing. Therefore, they requested to be subsidized as well, at least 16 yuan per month, and also requested to reform the performance evaluation system.

Declaration of Strike: There are a total of 154 clerical staff in the two radio stations. On the 26th of this month, they jointly submitted a request to the heads of each station to forward the request for reform of the subsidy and performance evaluation to the Ministry. However, no reply has been received since the submission. The staff believe that the Ministry does not agree to their request, so they left the office at 0:05 this morning during the shift change and declared a strike.

Telegraph Service Unaffected: Although the staff of the two stations had previously requested improvement, they had not received a message with a deadline for a reply, so they were not prepared in any way. However, the duties of the clerical staff are not very important. Before 7:00 AM yesterday morning, the technical and telegraphic staff temporarily took over their duties and urgently telegraphed the Ministry for instructions. Personnel were also drawn from the branch stations and the Da Bei, Da Dong, and Pacific Sanshui Electric Companies to cope with the situation. Therefore, the telegraph service was not affected.

Ministry Orders Strict Handling: The International Radio Station and the Shanghai Wireless Telegraph Office, after telegraphed to the Ministry for instructions at 0:15 AM yesterday morning, received a reply from the Ministry at 4:05 PM, which stated that the staff had gone on strike and that a notice should be published in the Shen Bao and Xin Bao newspapers on the same day, ordering the staff to return to their posts and continue to serve. If they fail to report by the deadline, they will all be removed and dismissed. After receiving the order, the two stations have decided to publish a notice today to summon them.

Employees' Attitude: According to the striking personnel, because the bureau did not give a responsible and concrete reply, their attitude is very firm. They have all signed their names, unanimously demanding five conditions. There is no background to the demands. The responsible personnel of the two stations are deeply aware of this, but if the incident is prolonged and expanded, the responsibility will be borne solely by the authorities.

Naval Veteran Du Xigui Dies of Illness in Shanghai

Remains Moved to International Funeral Parlor Yesterday

Funeral the Day After Tomorrow, Condolences from All Walks of Life

Admiral Du Xigui, after the outbreak of the Fujian Incident, led the students of the Mawei Naval Academy to Beijing, and then returned to Shanghai. He died of pneumonia in his Shanghai residence at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. Those who heard the news mourned his death. Yesterday morning, his family had moved his remains to the International Funeral Parlor, and the funeral is scheduled for the day after tomorrow. Condolences have been received from all walks of life. The details are as follows:

After Arriving in Shanghai: Du Xigui, principal of the Mawei Naval Academy in Fujian, left Fujian on the Sanbei Shipping Company's Wanxiang ship on the 25th of last month with all the students of the Naval Academy and the naval training camp soldiers. He arrived in Shanghai on the 27th and took the original ship to Beijing again on the evening of the 28th, placing all the students in the Naval Torpedo School to study, so that their studies would not be interrupted. After Du had settled the students, he arrived in Shanghai from Beijing by train on the 2nd of this month, residing in his private residence at No. 146, Lane 146, Fuli Road, French Concession.

Sixtieth Birthday Celebration: Du Xigui was 60 years old. He held his sixtieth birthday celebration in Shanghai on the 20th of this month. Naval units stationed in Shanghai and the generals of the ships stationed in Shanghai went to congratulate him because Du was a veteran of the Navy, such as Chen Jiliang, commander of the First Fleet of the Navy. The occasion was very lively that day. Du personally greeted the guests and his spirit was still strong. He was planning to return to Beijing to preside over the affairs of the Naval Academy after his birthday, but unexpectedly he fell ill, which is very sad.

Dies in Shanghai Residence: Although Du was old, his health was good. On the morning of the 25th of this month, he felt slightly unwell and had a severe cough. His sons immediately hired a doctor to treat him. He was diagnosed with pneumonia. His condition suddenly worsened on the 26th. Despite treatment by famous Chinese and Western doctors, he passed away at 2:00 PM on the 27th due to his old age, leaving behind one concubine and two sons. His eldest son and wife and concubines are all in Shanghai. His second son is in the Naval Academy in Beijing and immediately came to Shanghai to mourn upon receiving the telegram.

Funeral the Day After Tomorrow: After Du's death, his remains were transported to the International Funeral Parlor at No. 207 Jiaozhou Road yesterday morning. The funeral is scheduled to be held at 3:00 PM on the 31st of this month. Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sanctions Yongyichang Customs Broker for Reporting Substandard Newspaper Cargo

Shipped to Chongqing via Datong Steamer

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a report yesterday from the Paper Trade Association, stating that ten packages of Japanese newspaper, bearing the name "Meihua Trading Company of China," were declared by Yongyichang Customs Broker, located at Fushen Lane, Zhengjia Bridge, for shipment via the Datong steamer to Hankou, Yichang, and onward to Chongqing. The report requested that the Chamber of Commerce inform the Customs Broker Association to thoroughly investigate the consignor and strictly punish them as a warning. The Chamber of Commerce forwarded the letter to the Customs Broker Association for investigation, but the Association replied that Yongyichang Customs Broker was not a member of their association, and thus they were unable to conduct a thorough investigation into the declaration of substandard paper. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce responded with a stern letter, stating, "Although the firm is not a member, it is still in the same trade. It is difficult for it to escape the notice of the paper industry, and even more difficult to escape your Association's discerning eyes. While a thorough investigation may be difficult, a discreet inquiry is easier to undertake. As for punishing members, the most severe measures are fines or expulsion, all of which are sanctions on reputation. Yongyichang Customs Broker is in the same trade, and there must be business dealings between firms in the same trade. If you can admonish your members to regard them as public enemies in terms of morality and righteousness, cutting off dealings and stopping mutual assistance, the effect may surpass sanctions on reputation. Your Association's patriotism should be second to none, so there is no need to fear difficulty and shirk responsibility."

China National Aviation Corporation's Southwest Route Test Flight Canceled Yesterday Due to Fog

Test Flight to Begin Once Fog Clears in Changsha

In order to facilitate southwest transportation and meet the needs of Guangxi and Yunnan provinces, China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) is planning to open a southwest route from Hankou via Hunan, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Yunnan, to Chongqing. The test flight, originally scheduled to depart from Hankou yesterday morning, was canceled due to fog. Details are as follows:

Test Flight Plan: After completing the Shanghai-Peiping, Shanghai-Chongqing, and Shanghai-Guangdong trunk lines, CNAC began preparing to open the southwest route. In October of this year, two test flights were conducted from Chongqing, but both were aborted in Guiyang due to poor weather. Therefore, the plan was changed, with the flight departing from Hankou, flying to Changsha and then to Guangzhou, stopping overnight before flying to Wuzhou, Nanning, and then to Longzhou overnight. The next day, it would pass through Kunming and fly directly to Chongqing. If the weather is good, it may detour via Guiyang, as the climate along the entire route is most unfavorable in Guiyang. Therefore, it is planned that if the weather is bad, it will fly directly to Chongqing.

Test Flight Personnel: A Stinson aircraft will be used for the test flight, piloted by Chief Pilot Ericson. Accompanying him will be Mr. Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Aviation Department, and Mr. Huang Baoxian, Business Manager. It is said that Mr. Huang will remain in Guangzhou to investigate business conditions there. After the test flight is successful, the company will begin preparing for the opening of the route and plans to purchase new twin-engine aircraft for the line.

Postponed Due to Fog: The plane was scheduled to depart from Hankou yesterday (the 28th) morning, but due to heavy fog between Hankou and Changsha, the company decided to postpone the flight for safety reasons. The weather in the southwest is currently quite clear, and the test flight will begin as soon as the fog clears in Changsha.

China National Aviation Corporation to Increase Flights on Chongqing-Chengdu Section on New Year's Day

Four Times a Week on Tuesdays, Wednesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays

After the completion of the Shanghai-Chengdu route by China National Aviation Corporation, the Chongqing-Chengdu section was scheduled for flights from Chongqing to Chengdu on Tuesdays, Thursdays, Saturdays, and Sundays, once a day. A Heping News Agency reporter learned from the company yesterday that due to the increasing volume of mail transport on that section, the frequency of flights will be increased to four times a week, on Tuesdays, Wednesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays, starting on New Year's Day. The post office has been officially notified accordingly.

Ministry of Finance to Advance Payment of Government Bond Principal and Interest

To Be Paid by Designated Banks Starting on the 30th

The 31st of this month is the date on which the Ministry of Finance will begin repaying the principal and paying interest on various bonds. However, that day falls on a Sunday, and January 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of next year are New Year's holidays, during which banks will be closed for three days as usual. A Shenshi News Agency reporter learned yesterday that, in order to protect the interests of bondholders, the Ministry of Finance will advance the payment by one day to December 30th. A letter has been sent to the Government Bond Fund Management Committee for verification. The Committee, upon receiving the letter, has issued a public notice stating that the advance payment will be made on the 30th by the designated banks.

At the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association Central Auditorium and Lake Society

The War Zone Disaster Relief Association, in view of the suffering of the disaster-stricken people in the Northeast war zone, who are displaced, starving, and freezing, with the old and weak crying out in misery, which is unbearable to witness, has received repeated letters from the Northeast requesting relief. Monk Xuhui and others recently gathered colleagues to prepare relief. At this time of financial exhaustion, there is no good method. After discussion, it was decided to hold a variety show to raise funds for relief. It will be held during the year-end and new year holiday season when people from all walks of life are celebrating. It is learned that the association has made thorough preparations and will hold the show for four days, from the 31st to the 3rd, at the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association and the Central Auditorium and Lake Society. Invitations have been sent to various performing arts circles, all of whom have agreed to participate. The programs are all wonderfully exciting. Ticket prices are one yuan, two yuan, and five yuan. In addition to asking prominent figures to promote sales, tickets will also be sold at the venue, so that attendees can both fulfill their benevolence in helping and enjoy the fun of the show. It is expected that people from all walks of life will enthusiastically participate.

Poorhouse Sheltering Over a Thousand Destitute People

Borrowing Wood Planks to Build Additional Sheds

The Shanghai Charity Organizations United Association's temporary poorhouse in southern Shanghai, established on the 24th of this month, has sheltered general poor people and unemployed laborers. As of yesterday, the first location housed 269 people, the second location housed 516 people, and the third location housed 327 people, totaling 1,112 people. Shanghai gentlemen and merchants, such as Mr. Zhang Xiaoliang, mindful of the bankruptcy of the countryside and the decline of industry and commerce this year, with more unemployed people than in previous years, felt that the current location was insufficient. Yesterday, he borrowed a large number of wood planks from the Jiuji Lumber Company and the Zhenchang and Zhensheng Lumber Yards and sent them to the poorhouse to hire workers to build additional sheds, so as to maximize accommodation. Mr. Wang Yiting and Mr. Huang Hanzhi have raised funds from enthusiastic donors, including Mr. Pang Yitai, a benefactor, who donated 500 yuan, and the Pushan Villa, which donated 300 yuan. Mr. Lu Bohong has agreed with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to donate 200 yuan, which have all been sent to the association for the relief of poor people in the poorhouse. Mr. Gu Xinyi, a benefactor, felt that the poorhouse's rice consumption was very large and agreed to help purchase it on a voluntary basis.

Yesterday's General Meeting of the Bankers' Association

Passed the Final Accounts, Budget, and New Representatives

Banks Begin Closing Their Accounts Today

The Shanghai Bankers' Association held its fifth general meeting of members yesterday at 4:00 PM in the assembly hall of the association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. The meeting passed the final accounts for the current term, the budget for the next term, and the method for redeeming damaged exchange certificates. Details are as follows:

Representatives Present: Representatives from the following member banks attended: Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Real Estate Bank, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Salt Industrial Bank, Zhongfu Bank, Juxingcheng Bank, Siming Bank, China Bank, Guangdong Bank, Jin Cheng Bank, New China Bank, Donglai Bank, Continental Bank, East Asia Bank, Wing Hang Bank, China Industrial Bank, Sin Hua Trust, Zhongnan Bank, Overseas Chinese Bank, Jiangsu Bank, Guohua Bank, China Reclamation Bank, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Zhongxing Bank, Tonghe Bank, Hong Kong National Bank, China National Products Bank, and Central Trust, including Chen Guangfu, Bei Songsun, Ye Fuxiao, Chen Shuqing, Wu Yunzhai, Jing Runshi, Du Yuesheng, Yang Dunfu, Xu Jigu, Bei Lusun, Yang Jiemei, Xu Xinliu, Xu Zhonglin, Chen Guohua, Qu Jigang, Yao Yinpeng, Sun Hengfu, Zhu Zikui, Yuan Huiren, Wang Zhixin, Zhang Gongquan, and Feng Zhongqing, totaling 68 people. Secretary-General Lin Kanghou was present as an observer.

Chairman's Report: There are a total of 133 representatives from member banks. By 4:10 PM, 68 people were present, which was sufficient to meet the quorum. The meeting was declared open, and Chairman Chen Guangfu gave a report on the association's affairs after performing the formalities, including (1) discussing opinions on the Savings Bank Law, (2) unifying bank holiday dates, (3) establishing warehouse operating rules, and (4) studying opinions on revisions to the Negotiable Instruments Law. A printed copy of the association's affairs was distributed to the attending representatives of member banks.

Resolutions Passed: After the chairman's report, discussions began. The resolutions passed are as follows: (1) passed the final accounts for the current term and the budget for the next term of the 23rd year of the Republic; (2) passed the replacement of member representatives from China Industrial Bank and Juxingcheng Bank; (3) passed the admission of Chow Yieh Bank to the association; (4) passed the admission of Heng Lee Bank to the association; (5) passed ten articles on the method for redeeming damaged exchange certificates. The meeting adjourned at 4:45 PM.

Holiday Arrangement: The unified holiday arrangement of the Bankers' Association for the 23rd year of the Republic is as follows: (1) Sundays: Except for Siming Bank, China Bank, Wing Hang Bank, and Tonghe Bank, which will continue to operate as usual in the morning due to different business circumstances, all other banks will be closed. However, this does not apply to branches or offices of banks in the city that continue to operate as usual. (2) New Year's Day (National Calendar): January 2nd and 3rd. (3) Spring Festival: February 14th, 15th, 16th, and 17th. (4) Summer Holiday: June 16th. (5) Bank Half-Yearly Closing: July 1st and 2nd. (6) Autumn Holiday: September 23rd. (7) National Day: October 10th. The above table was drafted by the association. All member banks should take holidays according to the dates listed above. If any of the holidays from the 2nd to the 7th fall on a Sunday, one day should be added to the number of holidays on the day following the end of the holiday.

Annual Closing: Bank closing of accounts is conducted at the end of June and the end of December each year. The closing for the second half of the 22nd year of the Republic is December 31st. Since December 31st is a Sunday holiday this year, the bank closing of accounts has been advanced by one day, to December 30th. Today is December 29th, and the banks have already started processing the closing of accounts and extending working hours. Tomorrow, banks will extend their hours until dawn. The day after tomorrow, they will be closed.

Military Officer Becomes a Thief After Losing His Job

Robbery of Shanghai Bank Employee's Home for Jewelry

The Thief Studied Aviation Skills in Germany

Huang Shaoling, a 26-year-old Cantonese man residing at No. 33 Huaneng Road in the French Concession garden villa, a senior employee of two Shanghai commercial banks, was quite wealthy and newly married, possessing many precious items, thus arousing the covetousness of thieves. On September 22nd of this year, at around 10:00 AM, Huang went to work, and his wife also went out, leaving only his elderly mother and several maids at home. Suddenly, three thieves in Western suits, speaking with a Cantonese accent, rushed in through the back door under the pretext of delivering a letter. One thief held a handgun, and the other two held a long and short knife each. One thief monitored the homeowner's family and servants, while the other two went upstairs, looting cash, diamonds, jadeite, jade, gold ingots, and other various ornaments, totaling 10,000 yuan. After Huang found out upon returning home, he provided a list of the lost items, drew images of each item, and reported it to the police, requesting an arrest. Initially, the detective secretly investigated the maid Deng Er'a's whereabouts, but found nothing unusual. The detectives then sought external leads for the arrest. On the morning of the 22nd of this month, Chief Inspector Jin Jiulin of the special agency, leading detectives in conjunction with the Public Concession Police, arrested a Cantonese thief named Xu Shude (also known as Yin Jia), age 30, at Tianfu Lane on Laobazi Road. He was taken back to the police station, and the next day, he was escorted to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. After a detailed investigation by the police, Xu confessed that he had studied in Germany, where he attended the Berlin Aviation School. After graduating, he returned to China and served as an aviation combatant in the Army Department of Shanxi Province. In the 16th year of the Republic, he served as the commander and staff officer of the vanguard detachment. In the 19th year of the Republic, he left the military and came to Shanghai, where he worked as an actor for the Youlian Film Company. He was unemployed in July of this year and lived at No. 5 Funing Lane, Jiujiang Road. On the morning of September 15th, at 10:00 AM, a fellow villager friend, Wang Jing, came to visit and chat. I initiated the plan to rob the Huang family, and Wang agreed. Thus, on the morning of the 22nd of that month, at 8:00 AM, we opened a room at the Nanjing Hotel on Sanma Road to meet. Wang came with his friends Mai and Yazhu. Wang gave me a knife. Wang waited at the hotel, and I went to Huang's house with Mai and Ya to commit the robbery. I monitored the homeowner's family, and Mai and Ya committed the robbery. After returning to the Nanjing Hotel, we divided the loot. Wang made the assignments, and I received 300 yuan in cash, a pearl ring, a diamond ring, a gold hairpin, a gold cross, and other items, totaling 19 items. I then scattered and pawned them, using the money for expenses. When I returned from Nanjing, on the morning of the 22nd of this month, I went to the home of my friend Huang Zongru at No. 25 Tianfu Lane, Laobazi Road, to borrow travel expenses and was arrested when I arrived at the alley entrance. Based on his confession, the detective went to the Zikang Pawnshop at No. 553 North Sichuan Road, the Yuefeng Pawnshop on North Henan Road, and the Xiankang Pawnshop at the Eight Immortals Bridge, as well as the Dacheng Jewelry Store in Xiaguan, Nanjing, to retrieve the original stolen ornaments. Yesterday morning, Judge Li Changnian of the Second Special District Court interrogated him in the Criminal Court. Police lawyer Fei Xizhen stated the facts of the case and the police's investigation process and filed a public prosecution under Article 348 of the Criminal Law for robbery committed by a group of three. He also submitted the defendant's confession to the police station as evidence. Furthermore, Huang Shaoling's wife and her aunt arrived to testify about the robbery and requested severe punishment of the defendant and the recovery of the remaining stolen goods. When questioned, the defendant Xu Shude's testimony was the same as his confession to the police. He also stated that he lost his job due to the outbreak of the Shanghai Incident and, being troubled by food and clothing, was forced to take a risk and commit the crime. He requested lenient punishment so that he could still serve the country after being released from prison after serving his term. He referred to himself as a sinner and expressed deep hatred for the Japanese for invading Shanghai and causing him to lose his job and commit crimes. After reviewing the confession, the court appointed lawyer Wang Shizong to defend the defendant and then declared the debate closed. The sentencing was scheduled for the morning of the 30th, and the defendant was returned to custody to await instructions.

Dispute Over the Admission of Substandard Goods at the Yarn and Cloth Exchange

Not Meeting Appraisal Standards

Willing to Compensate Customers for Losses

The Shanghai Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange previously admitted substandard goods in October, disregarding the appraisal of the appraisers and damaging customers, causing customers to rise up in opposition, which caused a great storm and led to the resignation of all appraisers under their joint names, which caused the May floral auctions to not be held. And the customers had a meeting to vote to pursue them in court for fraud and breach of trust. It was previously reported. It is learned that the institution knew it was wrong, so it asked people to mediate and was willing to apologize to the customers and compensate them for more than 40,000 yuan to make up for their losses, so as not to cause a bigger storm. The organization also invited all the appraisers to dinner the night before to apologize and to discuss the resumption of the floral auctions in May. The results are unknown and will be tracked in the future. However, it is learned that some of the customers were able to accept the case because the end of the year was approaching, and they were afraid that their finances would be stranded. But some customers believed that the fraud and breach of trust by the organization was not appropriate, so they expressed their willingness to bear the losses and pursue the case in court to maintain the future of the customers and to warn others in the future.

British Employee of Jardine Matheson Commits Suicide

Leaving a Suicide Note Before Leaving

The Body Was Found on Tiyu Road

A foreign corpse, about 40 years old, wearing a gray woolen suit, was found in front of the empty house at No. 867 Tiyu Road, Jiangwan Road, at around 1:00 PM yesterday. Wang Jiufeng, the police chief of the Qujiaqiao Police Station in the fifth district of the Zhabei Municipal Public Security Bureau, found the corpse and immediately reported it to District Chief Jin Gong. After receiving the report, Jin sent personnel to investigate and found 23 yuan in cash, five English business cards, a bullet casing, and a gunshot wound on the chest of the deceased. The total situation was reported to the General Bureau for filing, and the district ordered the local security to request the court to examine the body in the afternoon. Reporters learned that the deceased was a British employee of Jardine Matheson at No. 27 the Bund. Before his death, the deceased left a suicide note on his desk in the office. After learning about the incident, the police took the corpse to the coroner's office on Feilun Road for examination.

Shooting on Shanhai Pass Road to Arrest Thieves, Stray Bullet Kills Driver

Two More Thieves Arrested at the Andong Hotel

Driver's Body Examined Yesterday Morning

At 11:30 AM the previous morning, three thieves from Suzhou, Zhou Yingen, Xu A'gen, and Qian A'mu, each carrying weapons, went out to rob. They first rented car No. 17708 from the Yitai Automobile Company on Hubei Road, driven by the driver Pan Lanfang. When they arrived at Shanhai Pass Road, they ordered the car to stop. Zhou and Xu got out of the car one after another and went to Wanchun Sauce Garden at No. 301 Shanhai Pass Road. Xu held a gun at the entrance to keep watch, and Zhou also held a gun and broke into the store, threatening everyone to remain silent. He robbed the shop of twenty-one yuan and thirty cents in large and small silver coins from the counter, as well as a gold ring from the finger of a woman, Wang Chenshi. He and Xu exited the shop, boarded the car, and tried to escape. At that time, Wang Chenshi's son, Wang Muxian, was also present. After the thieves left, he blew the whistle frantically and followed behind, reporting to the nearby station post Hua police No. 2976. After the police received the report and saw the car pass by, he immediately pulled out his gun and fired five shots. At this time, two other Hua police, No. 2763 and No. 882, hearing the gunfire, also assisted in the pursuit and fired two shots. The car's driver, Pan Lanfang, suddenly heard the whistle and gunfire and realized that the people in the car were thieves. Fearing harm from the thieves if he stopped the car, he unexpectedly jumped out of the car, but the car continued to move forward without a driver, crashing into a utility pole. The Hua police behind him were already following and boarded the car, arresting Zhou on the spot. The other two thieves escaped in the meantime. All of the stolen goods were found on Zhou, and a pistol was seized, with eight bullets inside. However, when the Hua police fired their guns, a cart driver from the Sanyou Company at No. 201 Shanhai Pass Road, Shen Yuxi, age 30, from Jiangbei, was passing by and was hit in the intestines by a stray bullet, damaging the large intestine. He fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. After the Xinza Police Station was notified, detective Ma Derong and a Western detective arrived and took the injured man to the hospital, but due to the severity of his injuries, he died at 1:30 PM. The body was sent to the Feilun Road coroner's office. Zhou Yingen was taken to the police station for questioning. Under interrogation, he admitted that he and the escaped Qian and Xu had committed the robbery and confessed that Xu and the others were hiding in Room 129 of the Andong Hotel on Hubei Road. Chinese and Western detectives went to arrest them, but Xu and the others had been there after the robbery, but had escaped five minutes earlier. So, detectives were stationed there. In the evening, two men from Anhui, Wang Chunfang, and a man from Zhejiang, Hong Yangbao, went to Andong 129 and were arrested by the detectives and taken to the police station for custody. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Court No. 8 of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated the previous situation and requested a postponement. Then, the Chinese and Western detectives and the victims Wang Chenshi and the witness Wang Muxian successively filed cases to prove everything. After Judge Xue Lanru briefly interrogated Zhou, Wang, and Hong, he ordered them to be detained for later questioning. Soon after, Prosecutor Diao Chengtang, appointed by the prosecutor's office of the Special Court, went to the office to examine the body of Shen Yuxi. After ascending to his seat, he interrogated again. Since he could not find any records of the body, he ordered Pushan Villa to collect the body on his behalf.

Opposition to Provincial Tax on Woodworking in the French Concession

Chen Juchang Would Rather Sacrifice Business

Small woodworking shops in the French Concession have never been subject to sanitation or business taxes. According to the regulations of the Public Works Department, only small industrial workshops with five or more employees are subject to taxation. However, this time, Chen Juchang's small woodworking workshop in Shenjiaqiao on West Pubuh Stone Road, which employs only three workers, unexpectedly received a notice from the Health Department last month, introducing a sanitation tax of two yuan per year. The workshop owner refused to pay the tax, as there had never been such a tax before, and was fined five yuan by the French police. However, he still refused to acknowledge the tax. Unexpectedly, he was summoned to the police station again and fined ten yuan. The workshop owner refused to comply and was prosecuted by the French police in the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. At the first trial, he was ordered to pay a fine of two yuan and obtain a permit from the Health Department of the French Municipal Council. The workshop owner argued that there was no such tax among his peers and that he should not be the first to acknowledge it, thereby disrupting industry regulations. He refused to accept the original judgment. Yesterday was the date for the second trial, and the Eighth Criminal Division again ruled that he must pay a fine of five yuan and apply for a permit from the Health Department of the French Municipal Council within ten days. The workshop owner still refused to comply and refused to sign the penalty. He then left the court and was given ten days to appeal. In order to fight for the interests of his fellow tradesmen, the workshop owner went to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association in the French Concession to report the circumstances of the court trial and his refusal to accept the penalty. After mediation by the association, it was found that the regulations of the Health and Business Tax of the French Municipal Council stipulated that, in addition to the previous court confirmation that those with five or more employees were subject to taxation and those with fewer than five were exempt, further reasons would be detailed and a request would be made to the court on his behalf for tax exemption. However, Mr. Chen Juchang, the workshop owner, is sixty years old and makes a living from this small woodworking business. If forced to comply, he would rather stop business operations and avoid the pain of excessive taxes and miscellaneous levies from his fellow tradesmen. The association specially offered comfort and encouragement, and Mr. Chen expressed his gratitude and said,

Public Buses in Zhabei Will Operate in the City Center Starting New Year's Day

Twelve Vehicles, Eight Already Fitted

Announcing Regulations for Routes, Fares, and Stops

The Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company, in response to the relocation of various bureaus of the new municipal government and the needs of people visiting, opened on the 20th of this month

The Fourth Public Bus Route Dedicated to the City Center

Started dispatching buses to operate in the city center, as reported in the newspapers. The company, to help the new urban area prosper, purchased twelve new-style Dæmon car chassis from the Yade Foreign Firm, rushed to process them, and installed the car bodies themselves. It is said that eight have been completed, with beautiful styles and comfortable seats. The car bodies use high-quality materials, and the outer walls are all made of lead-steel plates, which are very strong. The carriages are covered with artistic flower mirrors, which are extremely modern. The windows are soundproof, and the seat cushions are made of cowhide, all using domestic products. They are truly comparable to imported goods. The remaining four vehicles are still under construction. These eight new-style vehicles are scheduled to be officially put into operation on the fourth route on New Year's Day next year. The route and fare stops have been carefully approved by the authorities. The route starts from the Baoshan Road intersection, passes Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, Funei Road, Right Front Road of the Government, Houlu Road, and goes directly to the left side of the new Municipal Government building as the terminal. The driving time is from 7:00 am to 7:00 pm. Every Saturday and Sunday, it is extended to 10:00 pm. The fare stops are: from the North Station to Baoxing Road, 8 copper coins; to Tiantong Lane, 11 coins; to the Law School, 14 coins; to the Patriotic Girls' School, 17 coins; to Qujiaqiao, 21 coins; to Hechang Oil Factory, 24 coins; to the Animal and Plant Company, 27 coins; to Fudan University, 30 coins; to Guoding Road, 33 coins; to Songhu Road, 36 coins; to the First Park, 39 coins; to Fuxifu Road, 42 coins; to the Municipal Government, 45 coins. It is also reported that, if necessary, special buses may be added every day at 8:00 am and 5:00 pm. The full fare for the entire route is set at two jiao of small ocean.

Maritime Survey Bureau Notice to Ships

Radio Beacon Near the Mouth of the Yangtze River Damaged

The Hydrographic Office of the Navy Department announced that the radio beacon on Daji Mountain near the mouth of the Yangtze River has been damaged and its azimuth is temporarily suspended. The nearby lighthouse is located at approximately 122 degrees 10 minutes east longitude and approximately 30 degrees 49 minutes north latitude. All shipping companies were specially notified yesterday to pay attention.

Achievements of the Shanghai Mental Hospital

Shanghai is the first commercial market in East Asia, with a population of over three million. Only a few are in affluent circumstances. Recently, with the decline of the market and the withering of commerce, the number of unemployed people has increased sharply. Therefore, the strong take risks, and the weak suffer all kinds of stimulation. Some commit suicide, and some become insane. Mr. Gu Wenjun from Chuansha, sympathizing with the suffering of those who suffer from insanity, spent private funds to establish the Shanghai Mental Hospital in Ren'anli on Guling Road. Based on his ancestral secret recipe, he came out to help the world. In the half year since its opening, it has cured more than fifty men and women suffering from insanity. It is reported that those who have been cured and discharged from the hospital this month include Wang Zilin from Nanjing, 27 years old; Zhang Junsheng, a local, 23 years old; and Jiang Wang, a woman from Anqing, 50 years old. The above three people had been suffering from madness for many years and were sent to the hospital by their families for treatment one after another. They stayed for one or two months and were all cured and discharged from the hospital.

Invented by Art Printing Engineer Gao Yuanzai

Few printing plants in China have this machine. All Died One After Another a Few Days Later

Formerly a Student in the Nineteenth Route Army

Passed Through Hangzhou and Borrowed Travel Expenses

Found in a Yilinchun Teahouse

Stolen Goods and Guns and Bullets Seized

Patrol Leader Identifies and Sets a Date for Sentencing

Robbers Zhou Maoxian, Lin Xiaogui, and Wang Weichun from Jiangbei, along with a gang, robbed Zhou Bocheng's home at No. 4 Huatongfang, North Xizang Road, Yangzhou, on the morning of the 3rd of this month at 7:40 am, taking cash worth 43 yuan, gold rings, and other items. They fled after pushing open the door. When the Chinese and Western detectives from the Hongkou Police Station heard the alarm, they rushed to chase. The robbers fled wildly from Manzhou Road and Kulun Road in Zhabei. They were stopped by Zhang Liankui, Zhou Peixin, and Liu Qingxin, the police officers on duty in the fourth district. They opened fire and resisted arrest, and the three police officers were all shot and fell to the ground, taking the opportunity to escape without a trace. Afterwards, Patrol Leader Wu from the fourth district arrived and sent Zhang Liankui and others to Baolong Hospital. Police Officer Zhang suffered the most severe injuries and died at 1:00 am on the 8th. The three robbers, Zhou, Lin, and Wang, were arrested by Chinese Detective Chief Shi Sijian and Detective Bao Shuji from the Hongkou Police Station in the Yilinchun Teahouse on Jiujiang Road. A Mauser pistol used by Zhou to resist arrest, containing three bullets, and stolen goods, including two gold rings, were seized. They were sent to the First Special District Court for detailed interrogation. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan presided over the criminal court to investigate. The police lawyer Zhang Dayin stated that witnesses Zhou Shengpei and Patrol Leader Wu had arrived in court and requested questioning. According to Zhou, he was setting up a zifantuan stall in front of a coal store on Manzhou Road in Zhabei. At that time, he suddenly heard a police whistle and saw a police officer chasing a robber from Guoqing Road. He heard two gunshots. The police officer was shot in a vital part by the second shot and fell to the ground. He could not see the faces and figures of the robbers clearly. Patrol Leader Wu then testified that Police Officer Zhang Liankui said in the hospital that he was shot by a robber wearing a blue cotton robe and about 40 years old, which matched the defendant Zhou Maoxian. When questioned, the defendants' confessions were still the same as in the previous court hearing. Judge Wu ordered them to be returned to custody and set a date for sentencing.

Huanlong Road Fire

Yesterday morning at around 4:00 AM, a pile of rice straw belonging to Xu Maolang at No. 486 Huanlong Road in the French Concession caught fire, the cause of which is unknown. In an instant, thick smoke billowed and the fire raged. The fire brigade was alerted and rushed to the scene. They worked tirelessly to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished at 5:15 AM. Two bungalows were burned down.

No. 208

The Four Banks Reserve, jointly established by the Yanye, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks, specializes in issuing Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the reserve's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes is fully backed by reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guaranteed reserves accounting for up to 40%. A public announcement is made weekly.

Audited by the auditors and accountants of the Four Banks, the 208th public announcement of the Shanghai Reserve, dated December 23, 1933, is recorded as follows: Banknotes in circulation: 28,079,337 yuan. Total reserves: 28,079,337 yuan, including cash reserves of 22,233,887 yuan and guaranteed reserves of 5,845,450 yuan.

The Miraculous Effect of Contocalcium Powder - Medical scientists have long recognized calcium as suitable for treating numerous ailments. Contocalcium tablets, manufactured by the German Byk company, are a calcium preparation with an ideal formulation. Great care has been taken during manufacturing to consider factors such as the human body's ability to absorb organic and inorganic calcium, the influence of endocrine glands, and the action of vitamins. Therefore, its composition contains three different mixed calcium types, essential glands that aid development and digestion, and vitamins. After ingestion, it can be completely absorbed, allowing its valuable elements to fully exert their effects, mainly treating debility of all kinds, both internal and external, dental issues, as well as diseases of pregnant women and children. These tablets are delicious and palatable and have been sold in Germany and Europe for a long time with remarkable success. Now, the Shanghai-based Xinhua Company at No. 367 Jiangxi Road has been authorized as its distributor, with a constant stock of wholesale products available. They are also available in all major pharmacies.

Letter

To the Editor, Having read the news item titled "Tenants of Hexing Lane Oppose Rent Increase" in the local news section of your newspaper on the 28th of this month, we find it is inconsistent with the facts. Our accounting office proposed a rent increase this time to compensate for the sharp increase in donations, taxes, and water fees. This matter has been agreed upon with Xu Zhenya and Yin Changhuan, the fully authorized representatives of all the tenants in Hexing Lane, to increase the water fee, etc., by 20% of the original rent to show consideration. Unexpectedly, the news item stated that our accounting office colluded with the representatives using monetary means and that our agent, Lawyer Zhang Deqin, threatened Zhang Jinkui and Chen Ruzhang to withdraw from the agency relationship. Not only are the facts completely fabricated, but they are also deliberately damaging our reputation. Also, the news report on the mediation court situation changed the judge's in-court advice of "increasing the water fee, etc., by 20%" to "it is impossible to increase the rent." This is a distortion of the court record. In addition to Zhang Jinkui and Chen Ruzhang withdrawing from the representative relationship, there is an announcement on the cover of the Xinwen Daily, etc., on the 17th of this month, which can prove the truth. In addition to taking legal action on the part that damages the reputation of our accounting office, we are concerned about confusing the truth. Therefore, we have sent this special letter to you, hoping that your newspaper will correct it immediately to avoid confusion. Thank you very much. Sincerely, Deji Accounting Office, on behalf of the landlord. December 28, 1933.
